Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Classification (Already Performed)\n\nClassification was handled by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The tier has been determined and the classification header has been emitted. Proceed directly to execution based on the classified tier.\n\n**Reference** — the tier keyword tables (for context only, do not re-classify):\n- **STRICT**: security, authentication, database, migration, refactor, breaking change, encrypt, token, session, oauth\n- **EXEMPT**: explain, search, commit, push, plan, discuss, brainstorm\n- **LIGHT**: typo, comment, whitespace, lint, docstring, formatting, minor\n- **STANDARD**: implement, add, create, update, fix, build, modify, change (default)\n\n### 2. Confidence Display (Human-Readable)\n\nAfter the mandatory classification header, show a human-readable summary:\n\n```\n**Tier: STANDARD** [████████░░] 80%\n\nClassified as STANDARD:\n- Keywords matched: add, implement\n- Confidence score: 0.78\n- Considered alternatives: STRICT (0.35)\n```\n\nIf confidence <70%, add prompt: \"⚠️ Low confidence. This human-readable display is for user understanding.\n\n### 3. Execution Phase\n\nExecute task according to tier requirements:\n\n**STRICT Execution**:\n1. Activate project (mcp__serena__activate_project)\n2. Verify git working directory clean (git status)\n3. Load codebase context (codebase-retrieval)\n4. Check relevant memories (list_memories -> read_memory)\n5. Identify all affected files and test files\n6. Make changes with full checklist\n7. Identify all files that import changed code\n8. Update all affected files\n9. Spawn verification agent (quality-engineer)\n10. Run comprehensive tests: `pytest [path] -v`\n11. Answer adversarial questions\n\n**STANDARD Execution**:\n1. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 5. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. check\n\n## Examples\n\n### STRICT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"implement user authentication with JWT\"\n\n-> Classified as STRICT (security domain, authentication keyword)\n-> Full 6-category checklist enforced\n-> Verification agent spawned\n-> Adversarial questions answered\n```\n\n### STANDARD Task\n```\n/sc:task \"add pagination to user list\"\n\n-> Classified as STANDARD (add keyword, typical classification\n-> Full verification enforced\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Classify tasks into appropriate compliance tiers\n- Enforce tier-appropriate verification requirements\n- Provide `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/tests/roadmap/test_validate_gates.py`\n\nBehavior currently implemented:\n\n- Validation requires these prior-phase outputs in an output directory:\n  - `roadmap.md`\n  - `test-strategy.md`\n  - `extraction.md`\n- Single-agent mode:\n  - one `reflect` step producing `validate/validation-report.md`\n- Multi-agent mode:\n  - parallel `reflect-*` steps\n  - then `adversarial-merge`\n  - final output `validate/validation-report.md`\n- Partial multi-agent failure:\n  - degraded report is written instead of silent success\n- `roadmap run` auto-invokes validation unless `--no-validate`\n- Validation status is recorded in `.roadmap-state.json`\n- On resume, validation is skipped if already completed with `pass` or `fail`\n\n---\n\n# Full contents requested\n\n## `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_executor.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Validation executor -- orchestrates the validation pipeline.\n\nReads for validation\n_REQUIRED_INPUTS = (\"roadmap.md\", \"test-strategy.md\", \"extraction.md\")\n\n\ndef _embed_inputs(input_paths: list[Path]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Read input files and return their contents as fenced code blocks.\"\"\"\n    if not input_paths:\n        return \"\"\n    blocks: list[str] = []\n    for p in input_paths:\n        content = Path(p).read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n        blocks.append(f\"# {p}\\n```\\n{content}\\n```\")\n    return \"\\n\\n\".join(blocks)\n\n\ndef _sanitize_output(output_file: Path) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Strip conversational preamble before YAML frontmatter.\"\"\"\n    import os\n    import re\n\n    try:\n        content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    except FileNotFoundError:\n        return 0\n\n    if content.lstrip().startswith(\"---\"):\n        return 0\n\n    match = re.search(r\"^---[ \\t]*$\", content, re.MULTILINE)\n    if match is None:\n        return 0\n\n    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n    cleaned = content[match.start() :]\n    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n\n    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n\n    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n    return preamble_bytes\n\n\ndef validate_run_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single validation step as a Claude subprocess.\n\n    Mirrors ``roadmap_run_step`` from ``executor.py``: builds argv,\n    launches process, waits with timeout, sanitizes output.\n    \"\"\"\n    started_at = status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n        )\n\n    # Inline embedding\n    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n        extra_args: list[str] = []\n    elif embedded:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n\n    return StepResult(\n        step=step,\n        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n        attempt=1,\n        started_at=started_at,\n        finished_at=finished_at,\n    )\n\n\ndef _validate_input_files(output_dir: Path) -> list[Path]:\n    \"\"\"Validate that required input files exist, return their paths.\n\n    Raises FileNotFoundError if any required file is missing.\n    \"\"\"\n    paths = []\n    for name in _REQUIRED_INPUTS:\n        p = output_dir / name\n        if not p.exists():\n            raise FileNotFoundError(\n                f\"Required validation input not found: {p}\"\n            )\n        paths.append(p)\n    return paths\n\n\ndef _build_single_agent_steps(\n    config: ValidateConfig,\n    validate_dir:   model=config.agents[0].model,\n        ),\n    ]\n\n\ndef _build_multi_agent_steps(\n    config: ValidateConfig,\n    validate_dir: Path,\n    input_paths: list[Path],\n) -> list[Step | prompt=build_reflect_prompt(\n                    str(roadmap), str(test_strategy), str(extraction),\n                ),\n                output_file=output,\n                gate=REFLECT_GATE,\n merge_step = Step(\n        id=\"adversarial-merge\",\n        prompt=build_merge_prompt([str(p) for p in reflect_outputs]),\n        output_file=validate_dir / \"validation-report.md\",\n        gate=ADVERSARIAL_MERGE_GATE,\n        timeout_seconds=600,\n        inputs=reflect_outputs,\n        retry_limit=1,\n    )\n\n    return [\n        reflect_steps,  # parallel group\n        merge_step,     # sequential after all reflections\n    ]\n\n\ndef _parse_report_counts(report_path: Path) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Parse blocking/warning/info counts from a validation report's frontmatter.\n\n    Returns dict with blocking_count, warning_count, info_count.\n    Falls back to 0 for any unparseable field.\n    \"\"\"\n    result = {\"blocking_count\": 0, \"warning_count\": 0, \"info_count\": 0}\n\n    if not report_path.exists():\n        return result\n\n    content = report_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n        return result\n\n    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n    if end_idx == -1:\n        return result\n\n    frontmatter = content[3:end_idx]\n    for line in frontmatter.splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if \":\" not in line:\n            continue\n        key, _, val = line.partition(\":\")\n        key = key.strip()\n        val = val.strip()\n        if key == \"blocking_issues_count\":\n            try:\n                result[\"blocking_count\"] = int(val)\n            except ValueError:\n                pass\n        elif key == \"warnings_count\":\n            try:\n                result[\"warning_count\"] = int(val)\n            except ValueError:\n                pass\n\n    # Count INFO findings from body\n    body = content[end_idx + 4:]  # skip closing ---\n    info_count = 0\n    for line in body.splitlines():\n        if \"[INFO]\" in line:\n            info_count += 1\n    result[\"info_count\"] = info_count\n\n    return result\n\n\ndef _write_degraded_report(\n    report_path: Path,\n    failed_ids: list[str],\n    passed_ids: list[str],\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Write a degraded validation report when multi-agent validation partially fails.\n\n    The report is unmistakably marked as incomplete:\n    - YAML frontmatter with ``validation_complete: false``\n    - Prominent warning banner naming failed agent(s)\n    - Per OQ-2: \"Silent degradation is unacceptable.\"\n    \"\"\"\n    failed_list = \", \".join(failed_ids)\n    passed_list = \", \".join(passed_ids) if passed_ids else \"none\"\n\n    content = (\n        \"---\\n\"\n        \"validation_complete: false\\n\"\n        \"blocking_issues_count: 0\\n\"\n        \"warnings_count: 0\\n\"\n        f\"failed_agents: {failed_list}\\n\"\n        f\"passed_agents: {passed_list}\\n\"\n        \"---\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        \"> **WARNING: DEGRADED VALIDATION REPORT**\\n\"\n        \">\\n\"\n        f\"> The following validation agent(s) FAILED: **{failed_list}**\\n\"\n        \">\\n\"\n        \"> This report is INCOMPLETE. Findings from failed agents are missing.\\n\"\n        \"> Re-run validation to obtain a complete report.\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        \"## Status\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        \"This is a degraded validation report produced because one or more\\n\"\n        \"validation agents failed during multi-agent validation.\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        f\"- **Failed agents:** {failed_list}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Passed agents:** {passed_list}\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        \"## Findings\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        \"No consolidated findings available due to partial agent failure.\\n\"\n        \"Individual reflection files from successful agents (if any) are\\n\"\n        \"preserved in the validate/ directory.\\n\"\n    )\n\n    report_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    report_path.write_text(content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    _log.warning(\"Wrote degraded validation report to %s\", report_path)\n\n\ndef execute_validate(config: ValidateConfig) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Execute the validation pipeline.\n\n    Reads 3 input files (roadmap.md, test-strategy.md, extraction.md),\n    routes by agent count, applies gates, writes reports.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    config:\n        ValidateConfig with output_dir (containing pipeline outputs)\n        and agents list (1 agent = single mode, N = multi-agent).\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    dict with keys:\n        blocking_count: int -- total BLOCKING findings\n        warning_count: int -- total WARNING findings\n        info_count: int -- total INFO findings\n\n    Raises\n    ------\n    FileNotFoundError\n        If any of the 3 required input files is missing.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Validate inputs exist\n    input_paths = _validate_input_files(config.output_dir)\n\n    # Create validate/ subdirectory\n    validate_dir = config.output_dir / \"validate\"\n    validate_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n    # Route by agent count\n    if len(config.agents) == 1:\n        steps = _build_single_agent_steps(config, validate_dir, input_paths)\n    else:\n        steps = _build_multi_agent_steps(config, validate_dir, input_paths)\n\n    # Execute pipeline\n    results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n        run_step=validate_run_step,\n    )\n\n    # Check for failures and handle partial failure in multi-agent mode\n    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    report_path = validate_dir / \"validation-report.md\"\n\n    if failures and len(config.agents) > 1:\n        # Partial failure: some agents may have succeeded\n        failed_ids = [r.step.id for r in failures if r.step]\n        passed_ids = [\n            r.step.id for r in results\n            if r.status == StepStatus.PASS and r.step\n        ]\n        _log.error(\n            \"Validation partial failure: passed=%s, failed=%s\",\n            passed_ids,\n            failed_ids,\n        )\n        _write_degraded_report(report_path, failed_ids, passed_ids)\n    elif failures:\n        _log.error(\n            \"Validation pipeline halted: %d step(s) failed\",\n            len(failures),\n        )\n\n    return _parse_report_counts(report_path)\n```\n\n## `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_gates.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Validation gate criteria -- data definitions for validate pipeline steps.\n\nDefines GateCriteria instances for the validation subsystem:\nREFLECT_GATE and ADVERSARIAL_MERGE_GATE.\n\nImports from roadmap/gates.py only (unidirectional dependency preserved).\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom ..pipeline.models import GateCriteria, SemanticCheck\nfrom .gates import _frontmatter_values_non_empty\n\n\ndef _has_agreement_table(content: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check that content contains a markdown agreement table.\n\n    An agreement table has a header row containing 'agree' or 'agreement'\n    (case-insensitive) and at least one pipe-delimited data row.\n    \"\"\"\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    for i, line in enumerate(lines):\n        if \"|\" in line and (\"agree\" in line.lower() or \"agreement\" in line.lower()):\n            # Check for a separator row after header\n            if i + 1 < len(lines) and \"|\" in lines[i + 1] and \"-\" in lines[i + 1]:\n                return True\n    return False\n\n\nREFLECT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\n        \"blocking_issues_count\",\n        \"warnings_count\",\n        \"tasklist_ready\",\n    ],\n    min_lines=20,\n    enforcement_tier=\"STANDARD\",\n    semantic_checks=[\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"frontmatter_values_non_empty\",\n            check_fn=_frontmatter_values_non_empty,\n            failure_message=\"One or more required frontmatter fields have empty values\",\n        ),\n    ],\n)\n\nADVERSARIAL_MERGE_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\n        \"blocking_issues_count\",\n        \"warnings_count\",\n        \"tasklist_ready\",\n        \"validation_mode\",\n        \"validation_agents\",\n    ],\n    min_lines=30,\n    enforcement_tier=\"STRICT\",\n    semantic_checks=[\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"frontmatter_values_non_empty\",\n            check_fn=_frontmatter_values_non_empty,\n            failure_message=\"One or more required frontmatter fields have empty values\",\n        ),\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"agreement_table_present\",\n            check_fn=_has_agreement_table,\n            failure_message=\"No agreement table found -- adversarial merge requires an agreement/disagreement table\",\n        ),\n    ],\n)\n```\n\n## `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_prompts.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Validation prompt builders -- pure functions returning prompt strings.\n\nAll functions are pure: they accept concrete values, return ``str``,\nand perform no I/O, subprocess calls, or side effects (NFR-004).\n\nPrompt templates for the validate pipeline:\n- ``build_reflect_prompt``: single-agent reflection across 7 validation dimensions\n- ``build_merge_prompt``: adversarial merge with agreement categorization\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom .prompts import _OUTPUT_FORMAT_BLOCK\n\n\ndef build_reflect_prompt(roadmap: str, test_strategy: str, extraction: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Prompt for the 'reflect' validation step.\n\n    Instructs Claude to validate pipeline outputs across 7 dimensions\n    with BLOCKING/WARNING severity classifications.  Returns a structured\n    report with YAML frontmatter matching REFLECT_GATE criteria.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    roadmap:\n        Path (as string) to the merged roadmap file.\n    test_strategy:\n        Path (as string) to the test-strategy file.\n    extraction:\n        Path (as string) to the extraction file.\n    \"\"\"\n    return (\n        \"You are a validation specialist. You did NOT generate these artifacts.\\n\\n\"\n        \"Read the provided roadmap, test-strategy, and extraction documents. \"\n        \"Validate the roadmap across the 7 dimensions listed below. \"\n        \"Be thorough but precise -- false positives waste user time. \"\n        \"Every finding must cite a specific location (file:line or file:section).\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Validation Dimensions\\n\\n\"\n        \"Each finding MUST be classified as BLOCKING, WARNING, or INFO.\\n\\n\"\n        \"### BLOCKING Dimensions (failure = roadmap not ready for tasklist generation)\\n\\n\"\n        \"1. **Schema** -- YAML frontmatter fields present, non-empty, correctly typed.\\n\"\n        \"2. **Structure** -- Milestone DAG acyclic, all refs resolve, no duplicate \"\n        \"deliverable IDs, heading hierarchy valid (H2 > H3 > H4, no gaps).\\n\"\n        \"3. **Traceability** -- Every deliverable traces to a requirement AND every \"\n        \"requirement traces to a deliverable. Report untraced items.\\n\"\n        \"4. **Cross-file consistency** -- test-strategy milestone refs match roadmap \"\n        \"milestones exactly. No dangling references in either direction.\\n\"\n        \"5. **Parseability** -- Content is parseable into actionable items via \"\n        \"headings, bullets, and numbered lists by sc:tasklist's splitter.\\n\\n\"\n        \"### WARNING Dimensions (non-blocking but worth reporting)\\n\\n\"\n        \"6. **Interleave** -- Compute interleave_ratio using this formula:\\n\"\n        \"   `interleave_ratio = unique_phases_with_deliverables / total_phases`\\n\"\n        \"   (initial, subject to refinement)\\n\"\n        \"   Ratio must be in [0.1, 1.0]. Test activities must not be back-loaded \"\n        \"(i.e., concentrated only in the final phase).\\n\"\n        \"7. **Decomposition** -- Flag compound deliverables that would need splitting \"\n        \"by sc:tasklist. A deliverable is compound if it describes multiple distinct \"\n        \"outputs or actions joined by 'and'/'or'.\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Output Format\\n\\n\"\n        \"Your output MUST begin with YAML frontmatter delimited by --- lines containing:\\n\"\n        \"- blocking_issues_count: (integer) total number of BLOCKING findings\\n\"\n        \"- warnings_count: (integer) total number of WARNING findings\\n\"\n        \"- tasklist_ready: (boolean) true ONLY if blocking_issues_count == 0\\n\\n\"\n        \"After the frontmatter, provide:\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Findings\\n\\n\"\n        \"For each finding, provide:\\n\"\n        \"- **[BLOCKING|WARNING|INFO]** Dimension name: Description\\n\"\n        \"  - Location: file:line or file:section\\n\"\n        \"  - Evidence: what was expected vs. what was found\\n\"\n        \"  - Fix guidance: concrete steps to resolve\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Summary\\n\\n\"\n        \"Total counts by severity and overall assessment.\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Interleave Ratio\\n\\n\"\n        \"Show the computed interleave_ratio with the formula and values used.\"\n    ) + _OUTPUT_FORMAT_BLOCK\n\n\ndef build_merge_prompt(reflect_reports: list[str]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Prompt for the 'adversarial-merge' validation step.\n\n    Instructs Claude to merge multiple agent reflection reports into a\n    single consolidated validation report with agreement categorization.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    reflect_reports:\n        List of paths (as strings) to individual agent reflection reports.\n    \"\"\"\n    agent_count = len(reflect_reports)\n    return (\n        \"You are an adversarial merge specialist consolidating validation reports.\\n\\n\"\n        f\"Read the {agent_count} provided reflection reports from independent \"\n        \"validation agents. Merge them into a single consolidated validation report.\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Merge Categorization\\n\\n\"\n        \"For each finding across reports, categorize it as:\\n\\n\"\n        \"- **BOTH_AGREE**: Finding appears in both/all reports with consistent severity. \"\n        \"High confidence -- include in final report as-is.\\n\"\n        \"- **ONLY_A**: Finding appears only in Agent A's report. \"\n        \"Review recommended -- may be a true positive missed by other agents, \"\n        \"or a false positive.\\n\"\n        \"- **ONLY_B**: Finding appears only in Agent B's report. \"\n        \"Review recommended -- likely structural difference in analysis approach.\\n\"\n        \"- **CONFLICT**: Finding appears in multiple reports but with different \"\n        \"severity classifications. Escalate to BLOCKING.\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Agreement Table\\n\\n\"\n        \"Produce a markdown table with columns:\\n\"\n        \"| Finding ID | Agent A | Agent B | Agreement Category |\\n\"\n        \"|---|---|---|---|\\n\\n\"\n        \"Where Agent A/B columns show FOUND/-- and the category is one of \"\n        \"BOTH_AGREE, ONLY_A, ONLY_B, CONFLICT.\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Output Format\\n\\n\"\n        \"Your output MUST begin with YAML frontmatter delimited by --- lines containing:\\n\"\n        \"- blocking_issues_count: (integer) total BLOCKING findings after merge\\n\"\n        \"- warnings_count: (integer) total WARNING findings after merge\\n\"\n        \"- tasklist_ready: (boolean) true ONLY if blocking_issues_count == 0\\n\"\n        \"- validation_mode: adversarial\\n\"\n        f\"- validation_agents: (string) agent identifiers, e.g. 'agent-1, agent-2'\\n\\n\"\n        \"After the frontmatter, provide:\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Agreement Table\\n\\n\"\n        \"The categorized finding table as described above.\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Consolidated Findings\\n\\n\"\n        \"Merged findings list, ordered by severity (BLOCKING first, then WARNING, \"\n        \"then INFO). For CONFLICT items, explain the disagreement and your resolution.\\n\\n\"\n        \"## Summary\\n\\n\"\n        \"Total counts by severity, agreement statistics, and overall assessment.\"\n    ) + _OUTPUT_FORMAT_BLOCK\n```\n\n## `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/tests/roadmap/test_validate_cli.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Integration tests for CLI validate paths (Phase 4 for a generate step.\n\n    The model value is passed directly to ``claude -p --model``\n    (no resolution -- claude CLI accepts opus/sonnet/haiku natively).\n    \"\"\"\n\n    model: str\n AgentSpec.parse(\"opus:architect\") -> AgentSpec(\"opus\", \"architect\")\n            AgentSpec.parse(\"haiku\")          -> AgentSpec(\"haiku\", \"architect\")\n        \"\"\"\n        if \":\" in spec:\n            model, persona = spec.split(\":\", 1)\n            return cls(model=model.strip(), persona=persona.strip())\n        return cls(model=spec.strip(), persona=\"architect\")\n\n    @property\n    def id(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Short identifier for filenames, e.g. 'opus-architect'.\"\"\"\n        return f\"{self.model}-{self.persona}\"\n```\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass AgentSpec, ValidateConfig\n    from .validate_executor import execute_validate\n\n    # Default to 2 agents for roadmap-run auto-invocation (dual-agent for rigor per OQ-1)\n    validate_agents = work_dir=config.output_dir,\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=config.model,\n        debug=config.debug,\n    )\n\n    print(\"\\n[roadmap] Auto-invoking validation...\", roadmap execution.\n- `--resume` skips validation if prior validation status is already `pass` or `fail`.\n- Auto-validation uses up to the first two roadmap agents.\n- Missing required validation Create validate/ subdirectory\\n    validate_dir = config.output_dir / \\\"validate\\\"\\n    validate_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\\n\\n    # Route by agent count\\n    if len(config.agents) == 1:\\n        steps = _build_single_agent_steps(config, validate_dir, input_paths)\\n    else:\\n        steps = _build_multi_agent_steps(config, validate_dir, input_paths)\\n\\n    # Execute pipeline\\n    results = execute_pipeline(\\n        steps=steps,\\n        config=config,\\n        run_step=validate_run_step,\\n    )\\n\\n    # Check for failures and handle partial failure in multi-agent mode\\n    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\\n    report_path = validate_dir / \\\"validation-report.md\\\"\\n\\n    if failures and len(config.agents) > 1:\\n        # Partial failure: some agents may have succeeded\\n        failed_ids = [r.step.id for r in failures if r.step]\\n        passed_ids = [\\n            r.step.id for r in results\\n            if r.status == StepStatus.PASS and r.step\\n        ]\\n        _log.error(\\n            \\\"Validation partial failure: passed=%s, failed=%s\\\",\\n            passed_ids,\\n            failed_ids,\\n        )\\n        _write_degraded_report(report_path, failed_ids, passed_ids)\\n    elif failures:\\n        _log.error(\\n            \\\"Validation pipeline halted: %d step(s) failed\\\",\\n            len(failures),\\n        )\\n\\n    return _parse_report_counts(report_path)\\n```\\n\\n## `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_gates.py`\\n\\n```python\\n\\\"\\\"\\\"Validation gate criteria -- data definitions for validate pipeline steps.\\n\\nDefines GateCriteria instances for the validation subsystem:\\nREFLECT_GATE and ADVERSARIAL_MERGE_GATE.\\n\\nImports from roadmap/gates.py only (unidirectional dependency preserved).\\n\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n\\nfrom __future__ import annotations\\n\\nfrom ..pipeline.models import GateCriteria, SemanticCheck\\nfrom .gates import _frontmatter_values_non_empty\\n\\n\\ndef _has_agreement_table(content: str) -> bool:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Check that content contains a markdown agreement table.\\n\\n    An agreement table has a header row containing 'agree' or 'agreement'\\n    (case-insensitive) and at least one pipe-delimited data row.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    lines = content.splitlines()\\n    for i, line in enumerate(lines):\\n        if \\\"|\\\" in line and (\\\"agree\\\" in line.lower() or \\\"agreement\\\" in line.lower()):\\n            # Check for a separator row after header\\n            if i + 1 < len(lines) and \\\"|\\\" in lines[i + 1] and \\\"-\\\" in lines[i + 1]:\\n                return True\\n    return False\\n\\n\\nREFLECT_GATE = GateCriteria(\\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\\n        \\\"blocking_issues_count\\\",\\n        \\\"warnings_count\\\",\\n        \\\"tasklist_ready\\\",\\n    ],\\n    min_lines=20,\\n    enforcement_tier=\\\"STANDARD\\\",\\n    semantic_checks=[\\n        SemanticCheck(\\n            name=\\\"frontmatter_values_non_empty\\\",\\n            check_fn=_frontmatter_values_non_empty,\\n            failure_message=\\\"One or more required frontmatter fields have empty values\\\",\\n        ),\\n    ],\\n)\\n\\nADVERSARIAL_MERGE_GATE = GateCriteria(\\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\\n        \\\"blocking_issues_count\\\",\\n        \\\"warnings_count\\\",\\n        \\\"tasklist_ready\\\",\\n        \\\"validation_mode\\\",\\n        \\\"validation_agents\\\",\\n    ],\\n    min_lines=30,\\n    enforcement_tier=\\\"STRICT\\\",\\n    semantic_checks=[\\n        SemanticCheck(\\n            name=\\\"frontmatter_values_non_empty\\\",\\n            check_fn=_frontmatter_values_non_empty,\\n            failure_message=\\\"One or more required frontmatter fields have empty values\\\",\\n        ),\\n        SemanticCheck(\\n            name=\\\"agreement_table_present\\\",\\n            check_fn=_has_agreement_table,\\n            failure_message=\\\"No agreement table found -- adversarial merge requires an agreement/disagreement table\\\",\\n        ),\\n    ],\\n)\\n```\\n\\n## `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_prompts.py`\\n\\n```python\\n\\\"\\\"\\\"Validation prompt builders -- pure functions returning prompt strings.\\n\\nAll functions are pure: they accept concrete values, return ``str``,\\nand perform no I/O, subprocess calls, or side effects (NFR-004).\\n\\nPrompt templates for the validate pipeline:\\n- ``build_reflect_prompt``: single-agent reflection across 7 validation dimensions\\n- ``build_merge_prompt``: adversarial merge with agreement categorization\\n\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n\\nfrom __future__ import annotations\\n\\nfrom .prompts import _OUTPUT_FORMAT_BLOCK\\n\\n\\ndef build_reflect_prompt(roadmap: str, test_strategy: str, extraction: str) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Prompt for the 'reflect' validation step.\\n\\n    Instructs Claude to validate pipeline outputs across 7 dimensions\\n    with BLOCKING/WARNING severity classifications.  Returns a structured\\n    report with YAML frontmatter matching REFLECT_GATE criteria.\\n\\n    Parameters\\n    ----------\\n    roadmap:\\n        Path (as string) to the merged roadmap file.\\n    test_strategy:\\n        Path (as string) to the test-strategy file.\\n    extraction:\\n        Path (as string) to the extraction file.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    return (\\n        \\\"You are a validation specialist. You did NOT generate these artifacts.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Read the provided roadmap, test-strategy, and extraction documents. \\\"\\n        \\\"Validate the roadmap across the 7 dimensions listed below. \\\"\\n        \\\"Be thorough but precise -- false positives waste user time. \\\"\\n        \\\"Every finding must cite a specific location (file:line or file:section).\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Validation Dimensions\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Each finding MUST be classified as BLOCKING, WARNING, or INFO.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"### BLOCKING Dimensions (failure = roadmap not ready for tasklist generation)\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"1. **Schema** -- YAML frontmatter fields present, non-empty, correctly typed.\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"2. **Structure** -- Milestone DAG acyclic, all refs resolve, no duplicate \\\"\\n        \\\"deliverable IDs, heading hierarchy valid (H2 > H3 > H4, no gaps).\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"3. **Traceability** -- Every deliverable traces to a requirement AND every \\\"\\n        \\\"requirement traces to a deliverable. Report untraced items.\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"4. **Cross-file consistency** -- test-strategy milestone refs match roadmap \\\"\\n        \\\"milestones exactly. No dangling references in either direction.\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"5. **Parseability** -- Content is parseable into actionable items via \\\"\\n        \\\"headings, bullets, and numbered lists by sc:tasklist's splitter.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"### WARNING Dimensions (non-blocking but worth reporting)\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"6. **Interleave** -- Compute interleave_ratio using this formula:\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"   `interleave_ratio = unique_phases_with_deliverables / total_phases`\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"   (initial, subject to refinement)\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"   Ratio must be in [0.1, 1.0]. Test activities must not be back-loaded \\\"\\n        \\\"(i.e., concentrated only in the final phase).\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"7. **Decomposition** -- Flag compound deliverables that would need splitting \\\"\\n        \\\"by sc:tasklist. A deliverable is compound if it describes multiple distinct \\\"\\n        \\\"outputs or actions joined by 'and'/'or'.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Output Format\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Your output MUST begin with YAML frontmatter delimited by --- lines containing:\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- blocking_issues_count: (integer) total number of BLOCKING findings\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- warnings_count: (integer) total number of WARNING findings\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- tasklist_ready: (boolean) true ONLY if blocking_issues_count == 0\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"After the frontmatter, provide:\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Findings\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"For each finding, provide:\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- **[BLOCKING|WARNING|INFO]** Dimension name: Description\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"  - Location: file:line or file:section\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"  - Evidence: what was expected vs. what was found\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"  - Fix guidance: concrete steps to resolve\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Summary\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Total counts by severity and overall assessment.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Interleave Ratio\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Show the computed interleave_ratio with the formula and values used.\\\"\\n    ) + _OUTPUT_FORMAT_BLOCK\\n\\n\\ndef build_merge_prompt(reflect_reports: list[str]) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Prompt for the 'adversarial-merge' validation step.\\n\\n    Instructs Claude to merge multiple agent reflection reports into a\\n    single consolidated validation report with agreement categorization.\\n\\n    Parameters\\n    ----------\\n    reflect_reports:\\n        List of paths (as strings) to individual agent reflection reports.\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    agent_count = len(reflect_reports)\\n    return (\\n        \\\"You are an adversarial merge specialist consolidating validation reports.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        f\\\"Read the {agent_count} provided reflection reports from independent \\\"\\n        \\\"validation agents. Merge them into a single consolidated validation report.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Merge Categorization\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"For each finding across reports, categorize it as:\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- **BOTH_AGREE**: Finding appears in both/all reports with consistent severity. \\\"\\n        \\\"High confidence -- include in final report as-is.\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- **ONLY_A**: Finding appears only in Agent A's report. \\\"\\n        \\\"Review recommended -- may be a true positive missed by other agents, \\\"\\n        \\\"or a false positive.\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- **ONLY_B**: Finding appears only in Agent B's report. \\\"\\n        \\\"Review recommended -- likely structural difference in analysis approach.\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- **CONFLICT**: Finding appears in multiple reports but with different \\\"\\n        \\\"severity classifications. Escalate to BLOCKING.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Agreement Table\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Produce a markdown table with columns:\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"| Finding ID | Agent A | Agent B | Agreement Category |\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"|---|---|---|---|\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Where Agent A/B columns show FOUND/-- and the category is one of \\\"\\n        \\\"BOTH_AGREE, ONLY_A, ONLY_B, CONFLICT.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Output Format\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Your output MUST begin with YAML frontmatter delimited by --- lines containing:\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- blocking_issues_count: (integer) total BLOCKING findings after merge\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- warnings_count: (integer) total WARNING findings after merge\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- tasklist_ready: (boolean) true ONLY if blocking_issues_count == 0\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"- validation_mode: adversarial\\\\n\\\"\\n        f\\\"- validation_agents: (string) agent identifiers, e.g. 'agent-1, agent-2'\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"After the frontmatter, provide:\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Agreement Table\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"The categorized finding table as described above.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Consolidated Findings\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Merged findings list, ordered by severity (BLOCKING first, then WARNING, \\\"\\n        \\\"then INFO). For CONFLICT items, explain the disagreement and your resolution.\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"## Summary\\\\n\\\\n\\\"\\n        \\\"Total counts by severity, agreement statistics, and overall assessment.\\\"\\n    ) + _OUTPUT_FORMAT_BLOCK\\n```\\n\\n## `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/tests/roadmap/test_validate_cli.py`\\n\\n```python\\n\\\"\\\"\\\"Integration tests for CLI model:persona pair for a generate step.\\n\\n    The model value is passed directly to ``claude -p --model``\\n    (no resolution -- claude CLI accepts opus/sonnet/haiku natively).\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n\\n    model: str\\n    persona: str\\n\\n    @classmethod\\n    def parse(cls, spec: str) -> AgentSpec:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Parse a 'model:persona' or 'model' string into an AgentSpec.\\n\\n        Examples:\\n            AgentSpec.parse(\\\"opus:architect\\\") -> AgentSpec(\\\"opus\\\", \\\"architect\\\")\\n            AgentSpec.parse(\\\"haiku\\\")          -> 93→    if match is None:\n    94→        # No frontmatter found at all -- leave file unchanged\n    95→        return 0\n    96→\n    97→    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n    98→    cleaned = content[match.start() :]\n    99→    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   100→\n   101→    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n   102→    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n   103→    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   104→    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n   105→\n   106→    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n   107→    return preamble_bytes\n   108→\n   109→\n   110→def _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n   111→    output_file: Path,\n   112→    started_at: datetime,\n   113→    finished_at: datetime,\n   114→) -> None:\n   115→    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n   116→\n   117→    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n   118→    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n   119→    \"\"\"\n   120→    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   121→    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n   122→        return\n   123→\n   124→    # Find end of frontmatter\n   125→    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n   126→    if end_idx == -1:\n   127→        return\n   128→\n   129→    elapsed = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n   130→    diagnostics_line = (\n   131→        f\"pipeline_diagnostics: \"\n   132→        f\"{{elapsed_seconds: {elapsed:.1f}, \"\n   133→        f\"started_at: \\\"{started_at.isoformat()}\\\", \"\n   134→        f\"finished_at: \\\"{finished_at.isoformat()}\\\"}}\"\n   135→    )\n   136→\n   137→    # Insert before the closing ---\n   138→    new_content = (\n   139→        content[: end_idx]\n   140→        + \"\\n\"\n   141→        + diagnostics_line\n   142→        + content[end_idx:]\n   143→    )\n   144→    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   145→\n   146→\n   147→def roadmap_run_step(\n   148→    step: Step,\n   149→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   150→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   151→) -> StepResult:\n   152→    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n   153→\n   154→    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n   155→    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n   156→    \"\"\"\n   157→    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   158→\n   159→    if config.dry_run:\n   160→        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n   161→        return StepResult(\n   162→            step=step,\n   163→            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   164→            attempt=1,\n   165→            started_at=started_at,\n   166→            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   167→        )\n   168→\n   169→    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n   170→    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n   171→    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n   172→        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n   173→        extra_args: list[str] = []\n   174→    elif embedded:\n   175→        _log.warning(\n   176→            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n   177→            step.id,\n   178→            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n   179→        )\n   180→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   181→        extra_args = [\n   182→            arg\n   183→            for input_path in step.inputs\n   184→            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n   185→        ]\n   186→    else:\n   187→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   188→        extra_args = []\n   189→\n   190→    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n   191→        prompt=effective_prompt,\n   192→        output_file=step.output_file,\n   193→        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n   194→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   195→        model=step.model or config.model,\n   196→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   197→        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n   198→        output_format=\"text\",\n   199→        extra_args=extra_args,\n   200→    )\n   201→\n   202→    proc.start()\n   203→\n   204→    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n   205→    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n   206→        if cancel_check():\n   207→            proc.terminate()\n   208→            return StepResult(\n   209→                step=step,\n   210→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   211→                attempt=1,\n   212→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   213→                started_at=started_at,\n   214→                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   215→            )\n   216→        time.sleep(1)\n   217→\n   218→    exit_code = proc.wait()\n   219→    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   220→\n   221→    if exit_code == 124:\n   222→        return StepResult(\n   223→            step=step,\n   224→            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n   225→            attempt=1,\n   226→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n   227→            started_at=started_at,\n   228→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   229→        )\n   230→\n   231→    if exit_code != 0:\n   232→        return StepResult(\n   233→            step=step,\n   234→            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   235→            attempt=1,\n   236→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n   237→            started_at=started_at,\n   238→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   239→        )\n   240→\n   241→    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n   242→    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n   243→\n   244→    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n   245→    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n   246→        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n   247→\n   248→    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n   249→    return StepResult(\n   250→        step=step,\n   251→        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   252→        attempt=1,\n   253→        started_at=started_at,\n   254→        finished_at=finished_at,\n   255→    )\n   256→\n   257→\n   258→def _build_steps(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n   259→    \"\"\"Build the 8-step pipeline with parallel generate group.\n   260→\n   261→    Returns a list where 369→def _format_halt_output(results: list[StepResult], config: RoadmapConfig) -> str:\n   370→    \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n   371→    failed = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n   372→    passed = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.PASS]\n   373→    cancelled = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.CANCELLED]\n   374→\n   375→    if not failed:\n   376→        return \"\"\n   377→\n   378→    fail = failed[-1]\n   379→    step = fail.step\n   380→\n   381→    # Calculate file details if output exists\n   382→    file_info = \"\"\n   383→    if step and step.output_file.exists():\n   384→        content = step.output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   385→        byte_count = len(content.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   386→        line_count = len(content.splitlines())\n   387→        file_info = f\"  Output size: {byte_count} bytes ({line_count} lines)\\n\"\n   388→    elif step:\n   389→        file_info = \"  Output file: not created\\n\"\n   390→\n   391→    elapsed = f\"{fail.duration_seconds:.0f}s\"\n   392→\n   393→    lines = [\n   394→        f\"ERROR: Roadmap pipeline halted at step '{step.id}' (attempt {fail.attempt}/2)\",\n   395→        f\"  Gate failure: {fail.gate_failure_reason}\",\n   396→        f\"  Output file: {step.output_file}\",\n   397→        file_info.rstrip(),\n   398→        f\"  Step timeout: {step.timeout_seconds}s | Elapsed: {elapsed}\",\n   399→        \"\",\n   400→        f\"Completed steps: {', '.join(f'{r.step.id} (PASS, attempt {r.attempt})' for r in passed) or 'none'}\",\n   401→        f\"Failed step:     {step.id} ({fail.status.value}, attempt {fail.attempt})\",\n   402→    ]\n   403→\n   404→    # Collect skipped steps\n   405→    all_step_ids = _get_all_step_ids(config)\n   406→    executed_ids = {r.step.id for r in results}\n   407→    skipped_ids = [sid for sid in all_step_ids if sid not in executed_ids]\n   408→    if cancelled:\n   409→        skipped_ids = [r.step.id for r in cancelled] + skipped_ids\n   410→\n   411→    if skipped_ids:\n   412→        lines.append(f\"Skipped steps:   {', '.join(skipped_ids)}\")\n   413→\n   414→    lines.extend([\n   415→        \"\",\n   416→        \"To retry from this step:\",\n   417→        f\"  superclaude roadmap run {config.spec_file} --resume\",\n   418→        \"\",\n   419→        \"To inspect the failing output:\",\n   420→        f\"  cat {step.output_file}\",\n   421→    ])\n   422→\n   423→    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n   424→\n   425→\n   426→def _get_all_step_ids(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[str]:\n   427→    \"\"\"Get all step IDs in pipeline order.\"\"\"\n   428→    agent_a = config.agents[0]\n   429→    agent_b = config.agents[1] if len(config.agents) > 1 else config.agents[0]\n   430→    return [\n   431→        \"extract\",\n   432→        f\"generate-{agent_a.id}\",\n   433→        f\"generate-{agent_b.id}\",\n   434→        \"diff\",\n   435→        \"debate\",\n   436→        \"score\",\n   437→        \"merge\",\n   438→        \"test-strategy\",\n   439→    ]\n   440→\n   441→\n   442→def _print_step_start(step: Step) -> None:\n   443→    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step starts.\"\"\"\n   444→    print(f\"[roadmap] Starting step: {step.id}\", flush=True)\n   445→\n   446→\n   447→def _print_step_complete(step: Step, result: StepResult) -> None:\n   448→    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step completes.\"\"\"\n   449→    duration = {result.gate_failure_reason}\", flush=True)\n   462→\n   463→\n   464→def _dry_run_output(steps: list[Step | list[Step]]) -> None:\n   465→    \"\"\"Print step plan and gate criteria for 494→\n   495→\n   496→def _save_state(config: RoadmapConfig, results: list[StepResult]) -> None:\n   497→    \"\"\"Write .roadmap-state.json to output_dir via atomic tmp + os.replace().\n   498→\n   499→    Preserves existing ``validation`` key if present (written by\n   500→    ``_save_validation_status``).\n   501→    \"\"\"\n   502→    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n 529→    if existing_validation is not None:\n   530→        state[\"validation\"] = existing_validation\n   531→\n   532→    write_state(state, state_file)\n   533→\n   534→\n   535→def write_state(state: dict, path: Path) -> None:\n   536→    \"\"\"Write state dict to path atomically via tmp file + os.replace().\"\"\"\n   537→    import os as _os\n   538→\n   539→    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   540→    tmp = path.with_suffix(\".tmp\")\n   541→    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(state, indent=2), encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   542→    _os.replace(str(tmp), str(path))\n   543→\n   544→\n   545→def read_state(path: Path) -> dict | None:\n   546→    \"\"\"Read state from path with graceful recovery on missing/malformed files.\"\"\"\n   547→    if not path.exists():\n   548→        return None\n   549→    try:\n   550→        text = path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   551→        if not text.strip():\n   552→            return None\n   553→        return json.loads(text)\n   554→    except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):\n   555→        return None\n   556→\n   557→\n   558→def apply_decomposition_pass(deliverables: list[Deliverable]) -> list[Deliverable]:\n   559→    \"\"\"Post-generation decomposition pass for the roadmap pipeline.\n   560→\n   561→    Runs after deliverable generation, before output formatting.\n   562→    Splits behavioral deliverables into Implement/Verify pairs.\n   563→\n   564→    Idempotent: running twice produces identical results because\n   565→    already-decomposed deliverables (IDs ending .a/.b) are skipped.\n   566→\n   567→    Preserves milestone-internal ordering: deliverables within each\n   568→    milestone maintain their relative order after decomposition.\n   569→    \"\"\"\n   570→    return decompose_deliverables(deliverables)\n   571→\n   572→\n   573→def execute_roadmap(config: RoadmapConfig, resume: bool = False, no_validate: bool = False) -> None:\n   574→    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n   575→\n   576→    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n   577→    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n   578→\n   579→    After all 8 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n   580→    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n   581→    \"\"\"\n   582→    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   583→\n   584→    steps = _build_steps(config)\n   585→\n   586→    # --dry-run: print plan and exit\n   587→    if config.dry_run:\n   588→        _dry_run_output(steps)\n   589→        return\n   590→\n   591→    # --resume: check which steps already pass their gates\n   592→    if resume:\n   593→        from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n   594→\n   595→        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n   596→\n   597→    # Execute pipeline\n   598→    results = execute_pipeline(\n   599→        steps=steps,\n   600→        config=config,\n   601→        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n   602→        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n   603→        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n   604→    )\n   605→\n   606→    # Save state\n   607→    _save_state(config, results)\n   608→\n   609→    # Check for failures\n   610→    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n   611→    if failures:\n   612→        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n   613→        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n   614→        sys.exit(1)\n   615→\n   616→    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n   617→\n   618→    # Auto-invoke validation after successful pipeline completion\n   619→    if no_validate:\n   620→        print(\"[roadmap] Validation skipped (--no-validate)\", flush=True)\n   621→        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n   622→        return\n   623→\n   624→ 631→                print(\n   632→                    f\"[roadmap] Validation already completed ({saved['status']}), skipping\",\n   633→                    flush=True,\n   634→                )\n   635→                return\n   636→\n   637→    _auto_invoke_validate(config)\n   638→\n   639→\n   640→def _save_validation_status(\n   641→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   642→    status: str,\n   643→) -> None:\n   644→    \"\"\"Update .roadmap-state.json with validation status.\n   645→\n   646→    Adds or updates the ``validation`` key without modifying existing state.\n   647→\n   648→    Parameters\n   649→    ----------\n   650→    config:\n   651→        RoadmapConfig with output_dir.\n   652→    status:\n   653→        One of \"pass\", \"fail\", or \"skipped\".\n   654→    \"\"\"\n auto-invokes validation unless\n    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n    \"\"\"\n    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n    steps = _build_steps(config)\n\n    # --dry-run: print plan and exit\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _dry_run_output(steps)\n        return\n\n    # --resume: check which steps already pass their gates\n    if resume:\n        from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n\n        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n\n    # Execute pipeline\n    results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n    )\n\n    # Save state\n    _save_state(config, results)\n\n    # Check for failures\n    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    if failures:\n        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n\n    # Auto-invoke validation after successful pipeline completion\n    if no_validate:\n        print(\"[roadmap] Validation skipped (--no-validate)\", flush=True)\n        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n        return\n\n    # Check if validation already completed (--resume path)\n    if resume:\n        state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n        state = read_state(state_file)\n        if state and \"validation\" in state:\n            saved = state[\"validation\"]\n            if saved.get(\"status\") in (\"pass\", \"fail\"):\n                print(\n                    f\"[roadmap] Validation already completed ({saved['status']}), skipping\",\n                    flush=True,\n                )\n                return\n\n    _auto_invoke_validate(config)\n\n\ndef _save_validation_status(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    status: str,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Update .roadmap-state.json with validation status.\n\n    Adds or updates the ``validation`` key without modifying existing state.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    config:\n        RoadmapConfig with output_dir.\n    status:\n        One of \"pass\", \"fail\", or \"skipped\".\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    if state is None:\n        state = {}\n    state[\"validation\"] = {\n        \"status\": status,\n        \"timestamp\": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),\n    }\n    write_state(state, state_file)\n\n\ndef _auto_invoke_validate(config: RoadmapConfig) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Auto-invoke validation after a successful roadmap pipeline run.\n\n    Inherits --model, --max-turns, --debug from the parent roadmap config.\n    Default agent count for roadmap-run invocation is 2 (dual-agent for rigor).\n    \"\"\"\n    from .models import AgentSpec, ValidateConfig\n    from .validate_executor import execute_validate\n\n    # Default to 2 agents for roadmap-run auto-invocation (dual-agent for rigor per OQ-1)\n    validate_agents = config.agents[:2] if len(config.agents) >= 2 else config.agents\n\n    validate_config = ValidateConfig(\n        output_dir=config.output_dir,\n        agents=validate_agents,\n        work_dir=config.output_dir,\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=config.model,\n        debug=config.debug,\n    )\n\n    print(\"\\n[roadmap] Auto-invoking validation...\", flush=True)\n\n    try:\n        counts = execute_validate(validate_config)\n        blocking = counts.get(\"blocking_count\", 0)\n        warning = counts.get(\"warning_count\", 0)\n        info = counts.get(\"info_count\", 0)\n        print(\n            f\"[validate] Complete: {blocking} blocking, {warning} warning, {info} info\",\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        validation_status = \"fail\" if blocking > 0 else \"pass\"\n        _save_validation_status(config, validation_status)\n    except FileNotFoundError as exc:\n        _log.error(\"Validation skipped: %s\", exc)\n        print(f\"[validate] Skipped: {exc}\", file=sys.stderr, flush=True)\n        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n\n\ndef _apply_resume(\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    gate_fn: Callable,\n) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n    \"\"\"Apply --resume logic: skip steps whose outputs already pass gates.\n\n    Also checks for stale spec detection.\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    force_extract = False\n    if state is not None:\n        saved_hash = state.get(\"spec_hash\", \"\")\n        current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n        if saved_hash and saved_hash != current_hash:\n            print(\n                f\"WARNING: spec-file has changed since last run.\\n\"\n                f\"  Last hash: {saved_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"  Current:   {current_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"Forcing re-run of extract step.\",\n                file=sys.stderr,\n                flush=True,\n            )\n            force_extract = True\n\n    skipped = 0\n    result: list[Step | list[Step]] = []\n    found_failure = False\n\n    for entry in steps:\n        if found_failure:\n            # After first failing step, include all remaining steps\n            result.append(entry)\n            continue\n\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # Parallel group: check all steps\n            all_pass = True\n            for s in entry:\n                if s.gate:\n                    passed, _reason = gate_fn(s.output_file, s.gate)\n                    if not passed:\n                        all_pass = False\n                        break\n                else:\n                    all_pass = False\n                    break\n            if all_pass:\n                skipped += len(entry)\n                print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {', '.join(s.id for s in entry)} (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n            else:\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n        else:\n            # Force re-run of extract on stale spec\n            if force_extract and entry.id == \"extract\":\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n                continue\n\n            if entry.gate:\n                passed, _reason = gate_fn(entry.output_file, entry.gate)\n                if passed:\n                    skipped += 1\n                    print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {entry.id} (gate passes)\", flush=True)\n                    continue\n            found_failure = True\n            result.append(entry)\n\n    if skipped > 0:\n        print(f\"[roadmap] Skipped {skipped} steps (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n\n    if not result:\n        print(\"[roadmap] All steps already pass gates. Nothing to do.\", flush=True)\n\n    return result\n","numLines":783,"startLine":1,"totalLines":783}}}

The _parse_report_counts\n    function must correctly parse both fields so the invariant can be checked\n    by consumers.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def test_zero_blocking_means_ready(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"tasklist_ready should be true when blocking_issues_count == 0.\"\"\"\n        report = tmp_path / \"report.md\"\n        report.write_text(\n            \"---\\n\"\n            \"blocking_issues_count: 0\\n\"\n            \"warnings_count: 3\\n\"\n            \"tasklist_ready: true\\n\"\n            \"---\\n\"\n            + \"\\n\".join(f\"line {i}\" for i in range(25)),\n            encoding=\"utf-8\",\n        )\n        counts = _parse_report_counts(report)\n        assert counts[\"blocking_count\"] == 0\n        # Invariant: if blocking == 0, report should indicate readiness\n\n    def test_nonzero_blocking_means_not_ready(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"tasklist_ready should be false when blocking_issues_count > 0.\"\"\"\n        report = tmp_path / blocking_count == 0 iff tasklist_ready.\"\"\"\n        cases = [\n            (0, True),\n            (1, False),\n            (5, False),\n        ]\n        for blocking, expected_ready in cases:\n {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_01DrAyDnQHd8icawZvDW91td","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01KS316n2Qtmf6UCfP8XmsvY","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.dev/releases/current/v2.19-roadmap-validate/artifacts/D-0024/spec.md","content":"# Roadmap Validate -- Operational Documentation\n\n## Standalone Usage\n\nThe `validate` subcommand runs validation against existing pipeline outputs.\n\n```bash\n# Basic usage (single-agent, cost-efficient)\nsuperclaude roadmap validate ./output-dir\n\n# Multi-agent adversarial validation\nsuperclaude roadmap validate ./output-dir --agents opus:architect,haiku:qa\n\n# Custom model and debug logging\nsuperclaude roadmap validate ./output-dir --model sonnet --debug\n```\n\n**Required inputs**: The output directory must contain three files from a prior `roadmap run`:\n- `roadmap.md` -- the merged roadmap\n- `test-strategy.md` -- the test strategy\n- `extraction.md` -- the requirement extraction\n\n**Output**: Creates a `validate/` subdirectory containing:\n- `validation-report.md` -- the consolidated validation report with YAML frontmatter\n- Per-agent reflection files (multi-agent mode only): `reflect-{model}-{persona}.md`\n\n### CLI Options\n\n| Option | Default | Description |\n|--------|---------|-------------|\n| `--agents` | `opus:architect` | Comma-separated agent specs (model:persona) |\n| `--model` | (none) | Override model for all validation steps |\n| `--max-turns` | 100 | Max agent turns per subprocess |\n| `--debug` | false | Enable debug logging |\n\n## Multi-Agent Trade-Offs\n\n### Single-Agent Mode (1 agent)\n\n- **Cost**: ~1x token cost (one LLM call)\n- **Rigor**: Single perspective; may miss defects that another persona would catch\n- **Speed**: Faster (one subprocess)\n- **When to use**: Quick validation, cost-sensitive environments, iterative development\n\n### Multi-Agent Mode (2+ agents)\n\n- **Cost**: ~Nx token cost (N parallel reflections + 1 merge step)\n- **Rigor**: Multiple perspectives with adversarial merge; agreement categorization (BOTH_AGREE, ONLY_A, ONLY_B, CONFLICT) surfaces disagreements\n- **Speed**: Slower (parallel reflections + sequential merge)\n- **When to use**: Final validation before tasklist generation, high-stakes roadmaps, when confidence in roadmap quality is critical\n\n### Agreement Categories\n\n| Category | Meaning | Action |\n|----------|---------|--------|\n| BOTH_AGREE | Finding in all agent reports with consistent severity | High confidence -- include as-is |\n| ONLY_A / ONLY_B | Finding in one agent's report only | Review recommended -- may be true or false positive |\n| CONFLICT | Finding with different severity across agents | Escalate to BLOCKING |\n\n## --no-validate and --resume Interaction\n\n### Decision Matrix\n\n| Scenario | Validation Runs? | Notes |\n|----------|-----------------|-------|\n| `roadmap run spec.md` | Yes (auto-invocation) | Runs after all 8 pipeline steps pass |\n| `roadmap run spec.md --no-validate` | No | Records \"skipped\" in state file |\n| `roadmap run spec.md --resume` (all steps pass) | Yes | Auto-invokes after completion |\n| `roadmap run spec.md --resume` (step fails) | No | Pipeline halts with exit code 1 |\n| `roadmap run spec.md --resume` (validation already completed) | No | Skips with \"already completed\" message |\n| `roadmap validate ./output` | Yes (standalone) | Independent of pipeline state |\n\n### State File Interaction\n\nValidation status is persisted in `.roadmap-state.json` under the `validation` key:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"validation\": {\n    \"status\": \"pass\",\n    \"timestamp\": \"2026-03-08T12:00:00+00:00\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\nPossible status values: `\"pass\"`, `\"fail\"`, `\"skipped\"`\n\nThe `--resume` flag checks this state before running validation:\n- If `status` is `\"pass\"` or `\"fail\"`, validation is skipped (already completed)\n- If `status` is `\"skipped\"` or absent, validation runs normally\n\n## Default Agent Count Asymmetry\n\n### Standalone vs. Roadmap Run Defaults\n\n| Invocation | Default Agents | Count | Rationale |\n|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------|\n| `roadmap validate ./output` | `opus:architect` | 1 | Cost efficiency for ad-hoc validation |\n| `roadmap run spec.md` (auto-invocation) | First 2 from `--agents` | 2 | Higher rigor for pipeline completion |\n\n**Design decision (OQ-1)**: The asymmetry exists because:\n\n1. **Standalone validate** is often used iteratively during development. Running 2 agents each time doubles cost without proportional benefit when the user is actively fixing issues.\n\n2. **Roadmap run auto-invocation** happens once after all 8 pipeline steps complete. This is the \"final gate\" before tasklist generation, where the cost of missing a defect is higher than the cost of an extra LLM call.\n\n3. Users can always override: `--agents opus:architect,haiku:qa` works in both contexts.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1331,"cache_read_input_tokens":147786,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1331,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":24,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"9ea23731-d7c4-47e3-9481-8b7a04bbc09a","uuid":"ec3dbc37-12a7-4d09-a62b-d9c7b11cab3e"}

positive |\n| CONFLICT | Finding with different severity across agents | Escalate to BLOCKING |\n\n## --no-validate and --resume Interaction\n\n### Decision Matrix\n\n| Scenario | Validation Runs? | Notes |\n|----------|-----------------|-------|\n| `roadmap run spec.md` | Yes (auto-invocation) | Runs after all 8 pipeline steps pass |\n| `roadmap run spec.md --no-validate` | No | Records \"skipped\" in state file |\n| `roadmap run spec.md --resume` (all steps pass) | Yes | Auto-invokes after completion |\n| `roadmap run spec.md --resume` (step fails) | No | Pipeline halts with exit code 1 |\n| `roadmap run spec.md --resume` (validation already completed) | No | Skips with \"already completed\" message |\n| `roadmap validate ./output` | Yes (standalone) | Independent of pipeline state |\n\n### State File Interaction\n\nValidation status is persisted in `.roadmap-state.json` under the `validation` key:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"validation\": {\n    \"status\": \"pass\",\n    \"timestamp\": \"2026-03-08T12:00:00+00:00\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\nPossible status values: `\"pass\"`, `\"fail\"`, `\"skipped\"`\n\nThe `--resume` flag checks this state before running validation:\n- If `status` is `\"pass\"` or `\"fail\"`, validation is skipped (already completed)\n- If `status` is `\"skipped\"` or absent, validation runs normally\n\n## Default Agent Count Asymmetry\n\n### Standalone vs. Roadmap Run Defaults\n\n| Invocation | Default Agents | Count | Rationale |\n|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------|\n| `roadmap validate ./output` | `opus:architect` | 1 | Cost efficiency for ad-hoc validation |\n| `roadmap run spec.md` (auto-invocation) | First 2 from `--agents` | 2 | Higher rigor for pipeline completion |\n\n**Design decision (OQ-1)**: The asymmetry exists because:\n\n1. **Standalone validate** is often used iteratively during development. Running 2 agents each time doubles cost without proportional benefit when the user is actively fixing issues.\n\n2. **Roadmap run auto-invocation** happens once after all 8 pipeline steps complete. This is the \"final gate\" before tasklist generation, where the cost of missing a defect is higher than the cost of an extra LLM call.\n\n3. Users can always override: `--agents opus:architect,haiku:qa` works in both contexts.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
